# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
for (int i = 1; i <= n; ++i)
    fa[i] = i;

auto find = [&](int x)
{
    int u = x;
    while (u != fa[u])
        u = fa[u] = fa[fa[u]];
    return u;
}

int find(int u)
{
    return u == fa[u] ? u : (fa[u] = find(fa[u]));
}


void merge(int u, int v)
{
    int fu = find(u);
    int fv = find(v);
    if (fu == fv)
        return;
    if (sz[fv] > sz[fu])
        swap(fv, fu);
    sum[fu] += sum[fv];
    sz[fu] += sz[fv];
    fa[fv] = fa[fu];
} ^EmZZaoBG
